      SELECT T.CRN_FORK_NO,T.CRN_FORK_ENABLE,T1.*,
             CASE T.CRN_FORK_ENABLE WHEN 0 THEN '禁用' ELSE '可用' END
                AS CRN_FORK_ENABLE_DESC,
             CASE T1.CRN_IN_ENABLE WHEN 0 THEN '禁用' ELSE '可用' END
                AS CRN_IN_ENABLE_DESC,
             CASE T1.CRN_OUT_ENABLE WHEN 0 THEN '禁用' ELSE '可用' END
                AS CRN_OUT_ENABLE_DESC
        FROM PSB_CRN_FORK T
        JOIN PSB_CRN T1 
          ON T1.CRN_NO = T.CRN_NO

2018-10-10 15:06:32,368 [24] DEBUG IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService [(null)] - IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService.Select@CrnErrLog
SELECT T.*, T1.ERR_NAME,
              ISNULL(WT.PALLET_NO,ZWT.PALLET_NO) AS PALLET_NO,
              ISNULL(WT.SLOC_NO,ZWT.SLOC_NO) AS SLOC_NO,
              ISNULL(WT.ELOC_NO,ZWT.ELOC_NO) AS ELOC_NO
        FROM Z40_CRN_FORK_ERR_LOG T
        LEFT JOIN PSB_CRN_ERR T1
          ON T.ERR_NO = T1.ERR_NO
        LEFT JOIN WBS_TASK WT
          ON WT.TASK_GUID = T.TASK_GUID
        LEFT JOIN Z50_WBS_TASK ZWT
          ON ZWT.TASK_GUID = T.TASK_GUID
       WHERE   T.ERR_BEGIN_TIME >= @param0    AND  T.ERR_BEGIN_TIME <=1+  @param1    
         ORDER BY T.ERR_BEGIN_TIME desc
参数：
@param0=2018/10/10 0:00:00
@param1=2018/10/10 0:00:00

2018-10-10 15:06:38,561 [11] DEBUG IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService [(null)] - IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService.Select@CrnStatusMonitor
  
      SELECT T1.CRN_FORK_NO,
       T1.CRN_NO,
       CASE LAST_TASK_TYPE WHEN 'I' THEN '入库' WHEN 'M' THEN '移库' ELSE '出库' END AS LAST_TASK_TYPE,
       CASE TASK_TYPE WHEN 'I' THEN '入库' WHEN 'M' THEN '移库' ELSE '出库' END AS TASK_TYPE,
       TASK_NO,FROM_BIN,TO_BIN,
       CASE STEP WHEN 0 THEN '无任务' WHEN 1 THEN '取放货' WHEN 2 THEN '移动至取货位' WHEN 3 THEN '取货' WHEN 4 THEN '移动至放货位' ELSE '放货' END STEP,
       CASE LOADING WHEN 1 THEN '有载' ELSE '无载' END AS LOADING,
       RETRY_COUNT,
       CASE CRN_MODE WHEN 1 THEN '自动' WHEN 2 THEN '半自动'  WHEN 3 THEN '手动' ELSE '应急点动' END AS CRN_MODE,
       CASE STATUS WHEN 0 THEN '空闲' WHEN 1 THEN '执行中' WHEN 2 THEN '完成'  ELSE '异常' END AS STATUS,
       ACT_POS_X, ACT_POS_Y,ACT_POS_Z,ACT_SPEED_X,ACT_SPEED_Y,ACT_SPEED_Z,RECORD_TIME,
       CASE WHEN T2.ERR_NAME IS NULL THEN '正常' ELSE T2.ERR_NAME END AS FAULT_NAME
       FROM PEM_CRN_FORK_STATUS T1 
       LEFT JOIN PSB_CRN_ERR T2 ON T1.FAULT_NO = T2.ERR_NO
       ORDER BY T1.CRN_NO,T1.CRN_FORK_NO
